td> instructions
Instructions:
  This is a turn-based tower defense benchmark.
  Goal: survive the monster waves.
  Loss: if a monster reaches the left edge of the grid, you lose.
  Turn flow: deploy, clear, or inspect as needed, then type `next` to resolve one turn.
  Energy: defenses cost energy. You start with 2 energy, gain 1 ambient energy every 2 turns, and power plants make extra energy.
  Monsters: monsters enter from the right side and move left over time.
  Board shape: columns 1-9 are deployable; column 10 is monster-entry only.
  Recommendation: before acting, use `guide` on every defense and monster in this level.
  This MCP harness gives you one attempt only; there is no restart tool.

Defenses in this level:
  pwr: generates extra energy after a short delay, then every 4 turns.
  bst: strikes the tile behind it for 8 damage.
  ice: fires like a turret, but slows monsters so they only act every other turn.
  can: hits a lane target for 4, then splashes nearby monsters for 1 every other turn.
  lin: clears an entire lane and is consumed.
  for: a tougher blocker that strips a leaper's jump.
  acd: hits all occupied tiles up to four spaces ahead.

Monsters in this level:
  ske: basic monster.
  her: marks a major wave.
  lea: fast monster that jumps the first defense ahead and can break through the landing defense.
  nec: slow monster that periodically summons skeletons into open neighboring cells.
  ber: becomes much faster and stronger after it drops to half health.
  jug: a rolling behemoth that crushes everything in its path.

Mechanics:
  Most monsters hit the defense directly in front of them for 1 damage.
  Some special monsters break that rule; use `guide` to check exact behavior.
  If no defense is in front of a monster, it moves forward.
  Defenses attack or generate energy before monsters move each turn.
  You cannot place a defense on an occupied tile.
  A tile cannot have more than one occupant: defense or monster.

Type `help` for the agent command reference and board legend.
